Daakjenaar 27-Jun-18 02:53 AM
[OPEN RP] Cluster of abandoned Corpus cruisers orbiting Eris (4/02 A.R.)
There are lines no one should cross. Things that common sense dictates you to avoid. And for good reason, normally. The Technocyte should never be tampered with, even in ideal circumstances. And yet, there are those who choose to do so anyway.
~The hulking mass of this cluster of Corpus ships, melded together by Infested growths, was certainly hard to miss. The anonymous distress that led you all here seemed to be coming from the hangar of one of the ships toward the edge of the cluster, a smaller one mostly untouched by the Technocyte. The interior of the hangar seems just as untouched by it, with just a couple of small growths here and there. The hangar does look rather dillapidated, and probably hasn't been used in a few years. There is no sign of anyone being here since this ship was abandoned. No sign of any sort of distress call coming from here. Off in the distance, the growling of Infested can be heard, but that's nothing to be concerned about. Probably. For now, at least.~
Rozencratz - Sonera 27-Jun-18 04:58 AM
~A lone ships circles the cluster for what seems to be hours. The ship itself is small in craft, something akin to a Orbiter but of simple Corpus design and smaller in size. Dull white colors adorn it’s hull, accompanied by equally pale blue lines that drag out from the front to the back, marking it as if a huge beast clawed it down.~ ??? Finally, after all that mulling, scanning and thinking over, the craft dispatches a beat down Liset that slowly approaches the hangar of the least infested out of the brigade. With a hiss of air it enters the ships landing area, dropping down as gently as possible. The craft opens up and from it steps forth a very tall figure (1.86m) all dressed in dark traditional Arbiters robes and a dark blue colored cloak, his head wrapped in old bandages apart from a slit for his white eyes. There is a Silva & Aegis resting on his right arm and a single Viber by his left hip, along with a variety of gear items all lined up along his belt. A buzz rings out as his comms trigger “Are you sure about this?” A soft concerned voice speaks through “Keep a eye on the scans.” The figure replies in a commanding, muffled and robotic tone, not leaving room for any more discussion. He grabs on to his scanner and silently starts walking deeper in the interior, every sense on his body on high alert. He eyes the infested growths but mostly watches for any movement or indication of anyone still living – or not mutated. (edited)

Almighty_Jado - Kapak 29-Jun-18 09:51 PM
Kapak: "I'd almost forgotten how void-damn stupid this sector of space was," A Nidus cursed from within his Liset. The exterior of the ship was dented and warped, almost as if a massive hand had squished the metal hull in an giant grip before reshaping it back into its original form. Its paint job was faded, scratched, and flaking away, its original designs barely distinguishable against the uneven, asymmetrical bulges in the steel plates. The interior of the Landing Craft was just as bad, if not worse than the exterior. The walls were coated in strands of silk-like infestation, their ends snaking in and out of holes punched through the walls by the ravenous growths. The metal walls shared the same warped, misshapen features of the outside, and the atmosphere within the cabin was filled with orange spores that lingered hauntingly, like fiery snowflakes on a windless day. "It's been what, 4 years since I've been here?" Kapak asked, to no one in particular. His 'cephalon,' if you could call it that, remained quiet. It only spoke when spoken directly to, and kapak was mostly talking to himself to ease his nervous mind. "I hope Plaguewatch has moved the void out of here since then. Isn't anywhere else we can go to get what we need though, is there?" The ship creaked and groaned in response, sweat dripping from the muscular flesh that adorned the ceiling as the ship maneuvered around wreckage. Kapak paused though as a blip showed up on the ship's half-infested nav console. "A distress signal? Hmm. Probably just a technocyte colony that found a way to activate the beacon to lure travellers to their doom. Classic predatory move." Kapak remained quiet for a moment as the ship began to pass by the distress signal before he slammed his hand onto the powerless codex module. "FINE! OKAY!! WE'LL CHECK IT OUT!!" He slapped the surface again before pouting, arms crossed, his outburst directed at literally nothing. [1/2]
Kapak's Liset silently flew towards the ship before making a sharp turn upwards. The large Nidus just managed to squeeze himself through the Warframe deployment pod, popping loose and drifting through space until he reached the hull just above the hangar. He ripped open a servicing vault and pulled himself inside, working his way through the dark maintenance tunnel before finally plopping out onto a catwalk just above the previous two Tenno who had arrived. Muck. Tenno. Could have been worse I suppose, but also there's a good chance one of them knows who I am. Perhaps they're looking for the source of the signal as well...?
[2/2]
